To implement the task of setting up Google Document AI for extracting specified fields from supplier invoices, we will create a Python application with a graphical user interface (GUI). The application will use the Google Cloud Document AI API to process invoices and extract data, which will then be output in JSON or CSV format. We'll use the `tkinter` library for the GUI.

### Core Components

1. **Main Application (`main.py`)**: This will be the entry point of the application, handling the GUI setup and user interactions.
2. **Document AI Handler (`document_ai_handler.py`)**: This module will handle interactions with the Google Document AI API.
3. **File Processor (`file_processor.py`)**: This module will handle file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
4. **GUI Components (`gui_components.py`)**: This module will define the GUI components and layout using `tkinter`.

### File: `main.py`

This file will initialize the GUI and manage user interactions.

```python
# main.py

'''

Main application file for setting up the GUI and managing user interactions.

'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
from gui_components import create_main_window

def main():
    # Initialize the main window
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("Invoice Data Extractor")

    # Create main window components
    create_main_window(root)

    # Start the GUI event loop
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```

### File: `document_ai_handler.py`

This file will handle the interaction with Google Document AI.

```python
# document_ai_handler.py

'''

Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.

'''

from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'

        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()

        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )

        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return result.document

```

### File: `file_processor.py`

This file will handle file input/output operations.

```python
# file_processor.py

'''

Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.

'''

import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)

```

### File: `gui_components.py`

This file will define the GUI components using `tkinter`.

```python
# gui_components.py

'''

Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.

'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor

def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)

    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return

        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        document = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)

        # Extract fields (example)
        extracted_data = [{'field_name': 'value'}]  # Replace with actual extraction logic

        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)

        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")

    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)

    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()

    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)

```

### Notes

- Replace `'your_project_id'`, `'us'`, and `'your_processor_id'` with your actual Google Cloud project ID, location, and processor ID.
- Ensure you have the Google Cloud SDK installed and authenticated to use the Document AI API.
- The extraction logic in `process_file` should be replaced with actual logic to extract the necessary fields from the document.

**[Seminar Conclusion]**:

 To implement the task of setting up Google Document AI for extracting specified fields from supplier invoices, we will create a Python application with a graphical user interface (GUI). The application will use the Google Cloud Document AI API to process invoices and extract data, which will then be output in JSON or CSV format. We'll use the `tkinter` library for the GUI.

### Core Components

1. **Main Application (`main.py`)**: This will be the entry point of the application, handling the GUI setup and user interactions.
2. **Document AI Handler (`document_ai_handler.py`)**: This module will handle interactions with the Google Document AI API.
3. **File Processor (`file_processor.py`)**: This module will handle file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
4. **GUI Components (`gui_components.py`)**: This module will define the GUI components and layout using `tkinter`.

### File: `main.py`

This file will initialize the GUI and manage user interactions.

```python
# main.py

'''

Main application file for setting up the GUI and managing user interactions.

'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
from gui_components import create_main_window

def main():
    # Initialize the main window
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("Invoice Data Extractor")

    # Create main window components
    create_main_window(root)

    # Start the GUI event loop
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```

# file_processor.py

'''

Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.

'''

import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)

# gui_components.py

'''

Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.

'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor

def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)

    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return

        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        document = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)

        # Extract fields (example)
        extracted_data = [{'field_name': 'value'}]  # Replace with actual extraction logic

        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)

        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")

    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)

    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()

    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)

```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
# document_ai_handler.py
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return result.document
```

file_processor.py
```python
# file_processor.py
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
# gui_components.py
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        document = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Extract fields (example)
        extracted_data = [{'field_name': 'value'}]  # Replace with actual extraction logic
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

# document_ai_handler.py
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return result.document
```

# file_processor.py
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)

main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for setting up the GUI and managing user interactions.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
from gui_components import create_main_window

def main():
    # Initialize the main window
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("Invoice Data Extractor")
    # Create main window components
    create_main_window(root)
    # Start the GUI event loop
    root.mainloop()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)

    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor

def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)

    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")

    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)

    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor

def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)

    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")

    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

The correct client to use for processing documents with Google Document AI is `documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient`, not `documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient`, which is deprecated.

To fix this, update the `DocumentAIHandler` class as follows:

```python
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient()
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

The correct client to use for processing documents with Google Document AI is `documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient`, not `documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient`, which is deprecated.

To fix this, update the `DocumentAIHandler` class as follows:

```python
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)

    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor

def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)

    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")

    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")

    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)

    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data

class FileProcessor:

    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):

        if data:

            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

However, the highest priority issue is the hardcoded placeholders for `project_id`, `location`, and `processor_id` in the `process_file` function within `gui_components.py`. These should be dynamically set or configured through a configuration file or environment variables to ensure flexibility and security.

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Replace the hardcoded values with environment variables or a configuration file.
2. Update the `DocumentAIHandler` initialization in `process_file` to use these dynamic values.

Here's how you can implement this:

```python
# Import os module at the top of gui_components.py
import os

def process_file():
    file_path = file_label.cget("text")
    if not file_path:
        messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
        return
    # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
    project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
    location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
    processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
    
    if not project_id or not processor_id:
        messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
        return

    # Initialize Document AI handler
    document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
    extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
    # Save to JSON or CSV
    output_format = format_var.get()
    output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
    if output_format == 'json':
        FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
    elif output_format == 'csv':
        FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
    messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
```

Ensure that the environment variables `GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID`, `GOOGLE_LOCATION`, and `GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID` are set in your environment before running the application.

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id='your_project_id', location='us', processor_id='your_processor_id')
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

These should be dynamically set or configured through a configuration file or environment variables to ensure flexibility and security.

```python
# Import os module at the top of gui_components.py
import os

def process_file():
    file_path = file_label.cget("text")
    if not file_path:
        messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
        return
    # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
    project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
    location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
    processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
    
    if not project_id or not processor_id:
        messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
        return

    # Initialize Document AI handler
    document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
    extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
    # Save to JSON or CSV
    output_format = format_var.get()
    output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
    if output_format == 'json':
        FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
    elif output_format == 'csv':
        FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
    messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)

    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os

def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)

    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return

        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")

    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os

class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization

    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)

    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv

class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)

    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id

        # Read the file into memory

            image_content = image_file.read()

            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,

            )
        )

'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

'''
Main application file for setting up the GUI and managing user interactions.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
from gui_components import create_main_window
def main():
    # Initialize the main window
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("Invoice Data Extractor")
    # Create main window components
    create_main_window(root)
    # Start the GUI event loop
    root.mainloop()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

    # Start the GUI event loop

    main()
