document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data
```
file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)
```
gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

document_ai_handler.py
```python
'''
Handles interactions with Google Document AI API for processing invoices.
'''
from google.cloud import documentai_v1beta3 as documentai
import os
class DocumentAIHandler:
    def __init__(self, project_id, location, processor_id):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.location = location
        self.processor_id = processor_id
        self.client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient()  # Correct client initialization
    def process_document(self, file_path):
        # Set the processor name
        name = f'projects/{self.project_id}/locations/{self.location}/processors/{self.processor_id}'
        # Read the file into memory
        with open(file_path, "rb") as image_file:
            image_content = image_file.read()
        # Configure the request
        request = documentai.types.ProcessRequest(
            name=name,
            raw_document=documentai.types.RawDocument(
                content=image_content,
                mime_type='application/pdf' if file_path.endswith('.pdf') else 'image/jpeg'
            )
        )
        # Process the document
        result = self.client.process_document(request=request)
        return self.extract_fields(result.document)
    def extract_fields(self, document):
        # Extract specified fields from the document
        extracted_data = []
        for entity in document.entities:
            field_name = entity.type_
            field_value = entity.mention_text
            extracted_data.append({field_name: field_value})
        return extracted_data

file_processor.py
```python
'''
Handles file input/output operations, including reading images/PDFs and writing JSON/CSV outputs.
'''
import json
import csv
class FileProcessor:
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_json(data, output_path):
        with open(output_path, 'w') as json_file:
            json.dump(data, json_file, indent=4)
    @staticmethod
    def save_to_csv(data, output_path):
        # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries
        if data:
            keys = data[0].keys()
            with open(output_path, 'w', newline='') as csv_file:
                dict_writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=keys)
                dict_writer.writeheader()
                dict_writer.writerows(data)

gui_components.py
```python
'''
Defines the GUI components and layout using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from document_ai_handler import DocumentAIHandler
from file_processor import FileProcessor
import os
def create_main_window(root):
    # Create and place widgets
    def select_file():
        file_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf"), ("Image files", "*.jpg;*.jpeg;*.png")])
        if file_path:
            file_label.config(text=file_path)
    def process_file():
        file_path = file_label.cget("text")
        if not file_path:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please select a file first.")
            return
        # Retrieve configuration from environment variables
        project_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID')
        location = os.getenv('GOOGLE_LOCATION', 'us')  # Default to 'us' if not set
        processor_id = os.getenv('GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID')
        if not project_id or not processor_id:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Project ID and Processor ID must be set in environment variables.")
            return
        # Initialize Document AI handler
        document_ai_handler = DocumentAIHandler(project_id=project_id, location=location, processor_id=processor_id)
        extracted_data = document_ai_handler.process_document(file_path)
        # Save to JSON or CSV
        output_format = format_var.get()
        output_path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=f".{output_format}", filetypes=[(f"{output_format.upper()} files", f"*.{output_format}")])
        if output_format == 'json':
            FileProcessor.save_to_json(extracted_data, output_path)
        elif output_format == 'csv':
            FileProcessor.save_to_csv(extracted_data, output_path)
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", f"Data saved to {output_path}")
    # File selection
    file_label = tk.Label(root, text="No file selected")
    file_label.pack(pady=10)
    select_button = tk.Button(root, text="Select File", command=select_file)
    select_button.pack(pady=5)
    # Output format selection
    format_var = tk.StringVar(value='json')
    json_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="JSON", variable=format_var, value='json')
    csv_radio = tk.Radiobutton(root, text="CSV", variable=format_var, value='csv')
    json_radio.pack()
    csv_radio.pack()
    # Process button
    process_button = tk.Button(root, text="Process File", command=process_file)
    process_button.pack(pady=20)
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

```markdown
# Invoice Data Extractor

A Python-based application for extracting specified fields from supplier invoices in image or PDF format using Google Document AI. The extracted data can be saved in JSON or CSV format for database storage.

## Main Functions of the Software

1. **Invoice Data Extraction**:
   - Utilizes Google Document AI to process invoices in image or PDF format.
   - Extracts specified fields such as supplier name, invoice number, date, and total amount.

2. **File Format Support**:
   - Supports input files in PDF and image formats (JPEG, PNG).

3. **Output Options**:
   - Saves extracted data in JSON or CSV format, suitable for database storage or further processing.

4. **User-Friendly Interface**:
   - Provides a graphical user interface (GUI) for easy file selection, processing, and output format selection.

5. **Customizable Configuration**:
   - Allows users to configure Google Document AI credentials via environment variables.

---

## Installation Guide

### Step 1: Clone the Repository
Clone the project repository to your local machine:
```bash
git clone <repository_url>
cd <repository_directory>
```

### Step 2: Set Up Environment Dependencies
Install the required Python dependencies using `pip`:
```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

### Step 3: Configure Google Document AI
1. Set up a Google Cloud project and enable the Document AI API.
2. Create a Document AI processor for invoice processing.
3. Set the following environment variables with your Google Cloud project details:
   - `GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID`: Your Google Cloud project ID.
   - `GOOGLE_LOCATION`: The location of your Document AI processor (default is `us`).
   - `GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID`: The ID of your Document AI processor.

You can set these variables in your terminal or add them to a `.env` file for convenience.

### Step 4: Run the Application
Run the main application file to start the GUI:
```bash
python main.py
```

---

## How to Use the Application

1. **Launch the Application**:
   - Run the `main.py` file to open the GUI.

2. **Select an Invoice File**:
   - Click the "Select File" button to choose an invoice file in PDF or image format.

3. **Choose Output Format**:
   - Select the desired output format (JSON or CSV) using the radio buttons.

4. **Process the File**:
   - Click the "Process File" button to extract data from the selected file.
   - The application will use Google Document AI to process the file and extract specified fields.

5. **Save the Output**:
   - Choose a location and filename to save the extracted data in the selected format.
   - The application will notify you once the data is successfully saved.

---

## Example Workflow

1. Launch the application:
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```
2. Select an invoice file (e.g., `invoice.pdf`).
3. Choose the output format (e.g., JSON).
4. Click "Process File".
5. Save the extracted data to a file (e.g., `output.json`).

---

## Troubleshooting

1. **Missing Environment Variables**:
   - Ensure `GOOGLE_PROJECT_ID` and `GOOGLE_PROCESSOR_ID` are set correctly in your environment.

2. **Invalid File Format**:
   - Make sure the selected file is in PDF or image format (JPEG, PNG).

3. **Google Document AI Errors**:
   - Verify that your Google Cloud project is set up correctly and the Document AI API is enabled.

4. **Dependency Issues**:
   - Ensure all dependencies are installed using the provided `requirements.txt` file.

---

## Additional Notes

- This application requires an active internet connection to communicate with the Google Document AI API.
- For more information on setting up Google Document AI, refer to the [official documentation](https://cloud.google.com/document-ai/docs).

---

## License

This software is licensed under the MIT License. See the LICENSE file for details.
```
